        Distinct feature pools with limited overlap


ALTERNATIVE PATTERN (if a core exists):
â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•

Different outcomes draw on same feature pool

Cardiovascular outcomes:              Neurological outcomes:
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”          â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
â”‚ Age, Sex, BMI           â”‚          â”‚ Age, Sex, BMI           â”‚
â”‚ Smoking status          â”‚          â”‚ Smoking status          â”‚
â”‚ Townsend index          â”‚          â”‚ Townsend index          â”‚

â”‚ ...                     â”‚          â”‚ ...                     â”‚
â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜          â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜
        Near-identical despite distinct clinical domains

If so: Are outcome-specific features being systematically ignored?

â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•

\end{Verbatim}
~~~




### 8.3 Hypothesis: Wrong Features, Not Just Few Features


EPP constrains how many parameters can be estimated. It says nothing about whether the right parameters are being estimated.





~~~{=html}
<pre class="notion-ascii-diagram"><code>â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”

## 9. Medical Ontologies as Independent Benchmark


Medical ontologies (MONDO, HPO, EFO, ICD-10, SNOMED-CT) encode structured domain knowledge:


- Which biological processes relate to which diseases
- Which measurements reflect which physiological states
- Which features _should_ be relevant based on clinical/biological reasoning

This provides an independent reference point, separate from what papers actually use.



### 9.1 Example: Type 2 Diabetes




~~~{=html}

## 10. A Testable Research Framework


The EPP framework enables a specific, quantitative research programme:



### 10.1 Three Quantities to Compare




~~~{=html}
<pre class="notion-ascii-diagram"><code>â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”

â”‚        â†’ Extracted from: methods sections, supplementary materials      â”‚
â”‚                                                                         â”‚
â”‚    (c) DOMAIN EXPECTATION                                               â”‚
â”‚        Features suggested by medical ontologies for that outcome        â”‚
â”‚        â†’ Derived from: MONDO, HPO, EFO mappings to UKB fields           â”‚
â”‚                                                                         â”‚
â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜

\end{Verbatim}

### 10.3 Interpretation Matrix




~~~{=html}
<pre class="notion-ascii-diagram"><code>PATTERN                              INTERPRETATION

(b) â‰ˆ (a)                            Researchers operating at statistical
                                     limits. No evidence of underutilisation.

(b) &lt;&lt; (a) and (b) &lt;&lt; (c)            Systematic underutilisation.
                                     Statistical capacity is unused.
                                     Domain-relevant features ignored.
                                     â†’ STRONGEST EVIDENCE FOR PROBLEM

(b) &lt;&lt; (a) but (b) â‰ˆ (c)             Conservative but domain-appropriate.
                                     Using fewer features than possible,
                                     but aligned with domain knowledge.

                                     mis-specified. Operating at limits
                                     but feature choice may not match
                                     domain expectations.

## 11. Methodological Implications


### 11.1 What Finding a "Core" Would Mean


If analysis reveals:


- A small set of features (~50) accounts for majority of feature usage
- This set is stable across diverse outcomes (cardiovascular, neurological, etc.)
- Studies operate far below EPP capacity

Then we have quantitative evidence for systematic underutilisation â€” potentially a self-reinforcing pattern where researchers use familiar features regardless of outcome-specific relevance.



### 11.2 What This Does NOT Prove


Important limitations:





~~~{=html}
<pre class="notion-ascii-diagram"><code>â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
â”‚                                                                         â”‚
â”‚  EPP analysis can show:                                                 â”‚
â”‚    âœ“ Gap between capacity and utilisation                               â”‚
â”‚    âœ“ Whether feature usage varies by outcome                            â”‚
â”‚    âœ“ Degree of convergence on common features                           â”‚
â”‚                                                                         â”‚
â”‚  EPP analysis cannot show:                                              â”‚
â”‚    âœ— That unused features would improve prediction                      â”‚
â”‚    âœ— That commonly used features are wrong                              â”‚
â”‚    âœ— Causal relationships between features and outcomes                 â”‚
â”‚                                                                         â”‚
â”‚  The framework is DIAGNOSTIC, not PRESCRIPTIVE                          â”‚
â”‚                                                                         â”‚
â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜

## 12. Summary: EPP as Investigative Tool




~~~{=html}
<pre class="notion-ascii-diagram"><code>â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•

TRADITIONAL VIEW                      INVESTIGATIVE VIEW
â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€

&quot;Do I have enough events              &quot;Given available events, why are
 for my features?&quot;                     researchers using so few features?&quot;

EPP as constraint                      EPP as counterfactual

Protects individual studies            Characterises field-wide patterns
from overfitting                       of feature selection

Answers: &quot;Is this study               Answers: &quot;Is the field exploring
         adequately powered?&quot;                   available data?&quot;

â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•

The question is not just whether UK Biobank studies meet EPP thresholds.

The more interesting question:

  WHY DO THEY OPERATE SO FAR BELOW THEM,
  AND WHAT ARE WE POTENTIALLY MISSING AS A RESULT?

â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•
</code></pre>
~~~
